Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ВІЙНА', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'ҐВАЛТІВНИКИ РОСАРМІЇ', 'ОФІС ГЕНЕРАЛЬНОГО ПРОКУРОРА']

Category: News

Photo of the site Ukrinform.ua

Under the procedural leadership of the Kharkiv Regional Prosecutor's Office, the three -om Russian servicemen were informed in absentia of suspicion of violations and customs of war(Part 2 of Art. 28, Part 1 of Art. 438 of the Criminal Code of Ukraine).

Про цейдетьсяIn a message on the official prosecutor General's Office page on Facebook.

Law enforcement officers identified the military, which in the spring of 2022 raped a girl in Kharkiv. It is a 43-year-old colonel, commander of the 99-More Square Regiment of the 3rd Motorized Rifle Division of the 20-Rozagalian Army of the Western Military District of the Armed Forces of the Armed Forces and two of his subordinates: 20-year-old Private, which was a driver, and a 24-year junior sergeant, commander combat vehicle.

According to the investigation, the invaders came to the house where the family lives. At first, they threatened with weapons and then started shooting the tenses towards the outbuildings. After that, the suspects ordered them to give them all the means of communication for verification. Make sure that this civilianity, the Russian military left homeownership.

In the evening, they returned, ordered the girl's relatives to remain in all, and the victim was planted in the APC and taken to one of the houses where the commander was expected.

They closed the girl's eyes with a hooded so that she did not understand where she was being taken and not route. Along the way, the Russian military began to expose the girl.

When they arrived at the house where the commander was located, the invaders were roaring the girl. At the same time the commander told his subordinates that he would do it first.

After the de -occupation, the girl appealed to law enforcement agencies for the purpose of bringing the rapists.

The pre -trial investigation conducts the SBU.

Cannot be the norm of wars such as Russia is leading against Ukraine - the presidential speech at a joint meeting of the Senate and the House of Deputies of the National Congress of Chile

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-04-05T27:00:00-04:00

Description: Pan is head to the Senate, Pan's head of the Palator deputy!Inquiring for you for your words, for the take ... War with Ukraine 2022, war with Ukraine latest news today, news war with Ukraine 2022 The last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when, there will be a war with Ukraine in 2022 No, will there be a war with Ukraine in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukrainian news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['zelenskyj.jpeg', 'zelenskyj-1-150x150.jpeg', 'zelenskyj-2-150x150.jpeg', 'zelenskyj-3-150x150.jpeg']

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ВІЙНА', 'ВОЛОДИМИР ЗЕЛЕНСЬКИЙ', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'ПРЕЗИДЕНТ УКРАЇНИ', 'ЧИЛІ']

Category: News

Mr. Head of the Senate, Mr. Head of the House of Deputies!

Thank you for your words, for such a good greeting.

I see our flag in you. Thank you for respect for our flag, our hymn, to my state!

Ladies and Gentlemen!

Dear members of the National Congress of Chile, Dear Representatives and representatives of theiplomatic corps, dear journalists!

Chilean people!

Let me start my appeal from one story. From the story of the place in which the children were drawing.

Ordinary children, but unusual drawings. On the walls. At school. In the basement.

In the village of Yaidny in our Chernihiv region, where Russian soldiers were transformed a regular rural school for a concentration camp.

They drove all the villagers there. All!In the basement. Children and adults. Of completely years old people. Women and men. Less than 200 square meters per 360 people.

You may have not heard of this place yet. But I want to tell you about him.

To tell about the walls of this basement in the berry, on which the children painted that any children in any country: friends, relatives, their lives, their rivers, football players, other of their heroes.

The children tried to write the lines of our hymn, which just sounded here, the lines on the walls ... And the adults were calculating. Also on the walls. How many days ago, the basement and how many people were killed, not withstanding these conditions. Their cutters are still on those walls. I was there yesterday, I saw it all.

From the third to March 30 last year, the concentration camp in the berry existed.

At the beginning, people were still released outside. One at a time. Sometimes. At least in the toilet.

And then they were deprived of it. No minute of the sun and the sky. The basement of the basement, crushing, dust and bucket instead of the toilet.

We know exactly about the ten dead there. People just couldn't stand it. Know about those who were then shot in the village, who disappeared.

And I do not want to talk public now that the occupiers started to do, the outlings said that the dead had to be buried.

It was hell on the ground. Hell that came to Ukraine with the Russian army.

Perhaps somewhere on your continent, in some countries there are still positive nostalgic memories about the period of relations with the Soviet Union or the tour, which it pretended to be after 1991. But now this concentration camp characterizes who we are dealing with.

Why did you need such bullying? What could be a motive to keep the whole village in inhumane conditions in the basement?And when we turn to weapons partners, we only turn out. And nearly 1900 Ukrainian cities and villages, our soldiers managed to liberate the Occupation. Berry - among them.

Many villages, towns and cities have experienced even worse mockery. They are just burned.

Imagine a once strong village, for example, the post-Pokrovsky Kherson region of Ukraine, in which more than 2 thousand people lived, and now almost all homes are broken. If it is accurate, 96% of damage to shelling. That's it that Russia came!

Imagine when there are only 50 such almost completely broken by war in the region alone.

Imagine a city that has been famous for decades with its industry, with your naval port. And now the city is dead. Killed by Russia. This is our Mariupol.

!(Images/AРМІЯINFORM/2023-04-05T27-00-00-04-00/zelenskyj-1-150x150.jpeg)

Imagine one of the greatest Ukrainian values, one of the greatest human values - fertile fields that have been welfare for centuries. In the south country, in the east as well.

The fields that are now contaminated with Russian mines. Often, Russian missiles are protruding from this earth from the volley fire systems, reminding that one state's aggression against another cannot be justified.

Ladies and Gentlemen!

Chilean people!

Almost 1900 Ukrainian cities and villages should be liberated from Russian evil!

This is why we have created a coalition of countries that help Ukraine's defeat national independence and the lives of our people.

For this purpose, I offered the formula of peace last fall - ten points that can return Ukraine to Ukraine, and to all of Europe and all over the world - stability, violated by Russian fascism.

This is what we seek support to you - to the Chilean people.

Life has the same value everywhere. The highest value. There is nothing that could have been liable to destroy the lives of peaceful people, the humiliation of peaceful people, the subjugation of free peoples and robbery attacks on other states for profit.

I am grateful to you, Republic Chile, for the fundamental condemnation of Russian aggression, with the support of the relevant resolutions of the UN General Assembly.We form a global coalition to accomplish this and other similar tasks. And he is Yapti that we will fulfill them.

Everywhere in the world can not be the norm of burning cities and villages. There can be no normative, which someone wants to keep people in obedience. There can be no norm -concentration or filtration camps where people are driven and where people die.

The norms of wars as Russia now leads to Ukraine. And so, Russia itself, which it became, cannot and will not be the norm. It is a fascist state. State-Zlo. A state that deserves the legitimate and justification of the world is an attitude as a criminal.

Chilean people!

Ukraine invites you to join our peacekeeping efforts. Your voice in the Uonna Support for the Restoration of Ukraine's Security and Territorial Integrity is always very important.

Your participation in the implementation of our peace formula - which may not be a mere -human mineral demining - will accurately add an international order based on the rules.

I invite you to maintain our efforts for the food security of the world. This depends on the joint actions of all countries!

Due to the fact that the giant areas of our land are contaminated with mines or there are shelling, because Russia is blocking our ports and sea transportation to the Sea, the food market is destabilized.

We managed to unlock some of the supply. But the world needs more. Simply that the volume on the market and food prices on all continents are stable. You can be the leader of stabilization efforts from your continent!

Please support the efforts of the International Criminal Court, which has recently issued a warrant for the arrest of a Russian dictator in the case of the violent deportation of Ukrainian children into Russia and attempts to destroy their identity through assimilation and illegal adoption. With living relatives!

There is no such a crime that Russia would not have committed, conducting this war.

And there is no such people who could remain indifferent or neutral to evil.

Because we are all people. We all want the children of our peoples to be happy, security. They studied and rejoiced in life, not painted on the walls in captivity, in the cellars.

I thank you for your attention!Thank you for your support!

Let the dictatorship always lose, and life - always wins!

Thank you!

Glory to Ukraine!

Source: Presidential Ukrainian Official Internet.

In the Donetsk region in 21 settlements, forced evacuation of children - Irina Vereshchuk was announced

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-04-05T29:00:00-04:00

Description: PID Medicanes Vicepremere'yr-Ministra Irini Vereshchuk Vidbulo Zadydann Koordinaniye ... War with Ukraine 2022, War with Ukraine Latest news today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last for Ukraine and Russia, and when, the war with Ukraine in It will be or not, whether there will be a war with Ukraine in the near future, the war with Ukraine, Ukrainian news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian will be in Russian

Images: ['evakuacziya-ditej.jpg']

Tags: []

Category: News

Under the chairmanship of Viceremier Irina Vereshchuk, a meeting of the Coordination Headquarters was held on compulsory evacuation of the population of the martial law.

Coordination members unanimously supported the decision of the Donetsk OVA on the declaration of a compulsory evacuation of 126 children from 21 settlements of Donetsk region, the deny situation remains critical.

Currently, there are 5 evacuation crews of the White Angels. They ensure the safe removal of children on armored vehicles.

Evacuus children accompanied by one parent or a legal representative will be provided with free reflection, social guarantees, humanitarian assistance and psychological support.

For evacuation issues from Donetsk region, contact local departments or number:(098)890-33-18.

For the evacuation of seriously ill and persons with disabilities, please call:(099)710-48-72,(099)311-53-14,(099)311-53-36,(096)108-60-48,(096)108-52-24.

Source: Ministry of Reintegration of temporarily occupied territories

Category: News

The Cabinet of Ministers of Ukraine adopted a resolution that determines the response procedure for cyberincidents and cyber -attacks. This will allow you to react in a timely manner of cyber defense.

The first world cyber is now taking place. Therefore, it is extremely important to make the country's cyber resistance. To do this, you need to react in time and properly to cyberattacks to avoid negative effects. Defined order reacting will enable:

quickly identify and protect against cyberincidents or cyberattacks;

report the danger, prevent the negative effects or minimize them;

identify and correct vulnerability;

restore the sustainability and reliability of the functioning of information, electronic communication, information and communication, technological systems and other cyber defense.

Cyberattack response procedure and cyberincidents consists of several differenties: preparation, detection and analysis, restraint, elimination, restoration, analysis of the effectiveness of response measures. The resolution also defines criticality of kiberatak and cyberincidents.

The document was developed by the State Service of Special Communication and Protection of the Information of Ukraine for the implementation of the Cyber Security Strategy.

The World Bank expects that the growth of Ukraine's GDP in 2023 will reach 0.5% - the post -cutting fall to almost "minus" 30% according to the results of last year the post -start of the full -scale invasion of the Russian Federation into Ukraine.

“The amount of operations performed in Ukraine in the first place - payments made(107.0 trillion UAH, or 95.7% of all payments and transfers within Ukraine)”,- the report says.

Total number of participants in payment systems(In addition to the EPS)It is 132 financial institutions.

The patron sister will advise the family and assist the child's early development and possible risk of development; breastfeeding; immunization and prevention of infectious diseases; psychological problems in the family; a safe home environment for prevention of domestic violence; social problems.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-04-06T16:26:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-04-06T16:26:00+03:00

Description: In Sumy region, about a third of the 5,000 objects destroyed as a result of Russian aggression were restored for the year after the de -occupation. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16289...", "1680781747-96..."]

Tags: ['Будинок', 'Сумщина', 'Війна з росією', 'Відбудова']

Type: Article

The Sumy region, which has passed after the de -occupation, has been restored about a third of the 5,000 objects destroyed as a result of Russian aggression.

Taras Savchenko informed about it at a briefing at the Media Center Ukraine - Ukrinform.

"As of today, about 5 thousand different objects have been destroyed in the territory of Sumy region, and a third of them has been completely restored - about 1700 objects," Savchenko said.

According to him, among the list of affected structures, the largest private buildings are about 2,600. Their number increases in continuing arrivals by Russian troops of the Russian border communities in the region. There are also destroyed, educational institutions, apartment buildings, road and other.

Priority is the restoration of critical infrastructure: energy, water supply, bridges and more. At the same time during They also increase their level of defense to confront potential attacks.

The next is the restoration of apartment buildings. There are about 260 in the region, mainly in the territory of the Okhtyrsky district, which most complicated from hostilities.

Read also: Reconstruction "Regarding private homes, at the expense of the state program, which was approved last year, building materials were provided, the average communities were distributed, thus giving the opportunity to restore private homes," Savchenko said.

He stressed that there are several complex pro -correspondence of the central parts of the victims of settlements, in particular, in particular, in the Sumy region. The deputy manager said that the system compares the data and in the case of coincidence, police officers check them. After that, the persons whose data are running and proven by the police receive notifications and consent to the exchange.

"This can prevent, restrict or distort competition and influence consumer interests by limiting the import of motor fuel to the country," the commission was summed up.

The investigation of the CPC was focused on the behavior of "Lukoil Naftohim Burgas" and "Lukoil ”And found that the group has been granted the law, without giving importers and manufacturers of motor fuel to access the tax warehouses.

It is also noted that Lukoil has restricted imports of marine routes, blocked the warehouses related to the oil terminals of "Rosenets" and "Petrol-Varna" and not secured access to the petroleum products for transportation of fuel to other producers and importers.

The Lukoil group has the most extensive storage infrastructure in Bulgaria related to its transport infrastructure, and together with the high proportion of storage market of automobile fuel is the dominant enterprise of Ukraine.

However, according to the CPC, the group uses a strategy that includes several -competitive practices, which, in series and cumulative application for more than five years, create obstacles to fuel imports, or hinder this process, or making it economically ineffective.

According to the LUC, Lukoil abuses its dominance both under the law and EU legislation, since the restriction of imports into Bulgaria can significantly affect the scheme of trade in the Member States.

Type: Article

The International Monetary Fund provides for further "weak growth" of global economic economic in the conditions of continuation of the war of the Russian Federation against Ukraine, whose indicators, pronouns, will not exceed 3% this year.

This was stated on Thursday during a speech in Washington by the director of the IVFRKristalin Georgieva, reports his own correspondent of Ukrinform.

"Despite the surprisingly stable labor markets, as well as high consumer demand, renewal in China, we expect that the world economy will increase by a minor economy by 3%this year," Georgiev said.

She called it "historically weak growth" and noted that more details will be published in the review of the world economy next week, when the spring meetings will be used And the world bank.

Georgieva reminded that in 2021 the global economy showed a powerful growth, up to more than 6%. However, a significant shock from the War Solved by the Russian Federation, and its large -scale consequences significantly reduced this dynamics.

“Global growth in 2022 fell almost twice - from 6.1% to 3.4%. And the reappropriation will continue this year, ”she said.

The trade and economic relations between the EU and China are unbalanced and reflected, but the parties have huge volumes of trade, which last year amounted to more than 2.5 billion euros per day.

About it on Thursday in Beijing during a press conference following the meetings of the China's counterparts, the President of the European Commission Ursula von Der Lyen said, Ukrinform correspondent reports.

“The relationship between the EU and China has a great effect on the wealth and safety of both. For China, the European Union is the first(By value - ed.)export -string, while for the EU China is the third(The most important)export -bypass. To give a specific figure - the volume of trade was more than 2.5 billion euros a day in 2022, ”the President of the European Commission said.

At the same time, she acknowledged that bilateral trade relations are becoming more and more likely. Over the past 10 years, the Trade Bank Union in trade with China has increased more than three times and reached 400 billion euros last year. This topic was discussed today by the PRC, because, according to Ursula von der Lyen, such a trajectory is not a resistant and requires a systematic solution to structural problems.

In particular, the President of the European Commission has attracted attention to the fact that in China's European business is often faced with the practice of dishonest competition in some peasters and restricting access to European companies to the Chinese market. This applies to, for example, supplies of agricultural products from the EU, medical devices or other goods. Practically excluded from the PRC market the result of the discriminatory policy of the state "buy Chinese".

Read also: China These circumstances are also burdened with China's cross -border influences, in particular the requirements for the transmission of modern technologies, excessive number of information about a particular production, as well as improper protection of intellectual property in China.

All these circumstances are put by European companies that export to China, they have adjusted production in its territory, in unequal conditions with Chinese producers. This practice is a sharp contrast with the legal field that all companies use in a single EU market.She noted that there are different ways to reduce such risks. For example, to eliminate the risks associated with addiction, diversification of deliveries is used. In order to avoid the origins of the latest technologies, in particular, the defense sphere is to strengthen export control or screening. But in all cases, to solve the existing risks of the EU proposes the path of dialogue, the path of negotiations to find mutually acceptable solutions.

Read also: In order to solve these problems, according to Ursula von der Liaien, the EU and China, they have renewed high -level dialogue with economics and trade, as well as high -level dialogue in the digital sphere.

NASA Telescope made a new photo of Uranus

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-04-06T19:53:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-04-06T19:53:00+03:00

Description: James Webba NASA Space Telescope made a new detailed image of the Uranus planet. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_16687...", "1680799986-19..."]

Tags: ['Фото', 'NASA', 'Телескоп', 'Уран']

Type: Article

James Webba NASA Space Telescope has made a new detailed image of the planet.

As Ukrinform reports, it reports .

Data from the telescope demonstrate the unprecedented sensitivity of the observatory for the weakest dust rings of the planet. Their image was able to get only by stepping Voyager-2 ship in 1986 and Keck Observatory, which has advanced adaptive optics.

New Infrared Image from Clease Infrared Camera Chamber Webber(Nirkam)It combines data from two filters by 1.4 and 3.0 microns, which are shown in blue and orange, respectively. Uranus has blue -drawny in a representative color image.

Due to the infrared radiation and additional sensitivity of the telescope, the new image contains more details, showing the dynamics of the planet's atmosphere.

Also in the new photo can be seen bright clouds, which are generally typical of uranium in the infrared wave range, and are likely to be associated with shampower.

Uranus has 13 well -known rings, 11 of which are visible in a new image from telescowbba. Nine rings are classified as the main rings of the planet, and the other two are weaker rings.

Scientists expect that in the future, with the help of webba telescope, it will be possible to capture two weak external rings of the planet.

Read also: The photo also contains six of the well -known satellites of Uranus, which only holds 27.

James Webba Space Telescope is the world's main observatory in the world.

As reported , a group of scientists under the leadership of New York University Abu Dhabi(Nyud)and the Central Center for the United Arab Emirates created a new detailed map of the red planet thanks to the Hope Space Space.

Opto: NASA, ESA, CSA, STSCI. Image Processing: J. DEPASQUALE(STScI)

How to get aid to temporarily disabled workers during martial law

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Images: ['groshi.jpg']

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ВІЙНА', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ']

Category: News

About it reportsOmbudsman's office of Ukraine.

From January 1, 2023, the Pension Fund of Ukraine is an authorized body in the system of compulsory state social insurance. Accepted Ukraine No. 2620-IX “On Amendments to the Law of Ukraine“ ProZagal Compulsory State Social Insurance ”and the Law of Ukraine“ Protezological Compulsory State Pension Insurance ”, which provides for the connection of the Social Insurance Fund of Ukraine to the PFU.

In accordance with the Law of Ukraine "On Compulsory State Social Investment", insurance payment in connection with temporary loss of able-bodied persons working under the terms of an employment contract, a gig contract, other civil contract and on other ground carried out at the main place of work.

The right to insurance payments in connection with temporary disability are insured persons - citizens of Ukraine, foreigners, stateless persons of their families living in Ukraine, unless otherwise provided by the International Treaty of Ukraine.

The reason for the assistance of temporary disability assistance is a disability letter formed on the basis of a medical recovery on temporary disability or document certifying the child's factuality, establishing care over the child.

Temporary disability assistance is paid to insured persons depending on insurance experience in the amount of: In order to obtain funding for disability sheets from the PFU, the employer, which earlier, must submit an application containing the information performed by the insured persons. The terms of payments for hospital workers have not changed.

Payment of disability sheets is made, as it was before, 5 days of investment of own funds, starting from the sixth day - at the expense of insurance funds.

Please note that the PFU is financing the insurers within three work days after the application is received.

Importantly!The employer pays assistance for temporary disabled person in the nearest period of assistance, set for payment of wages.

It is a hotline on crisis issues, a hotline of IDPs' Ombudsman and the hotline of the Commissioner from missing.

The emphasis will be placed on housing, energy, critical, social and transport infrastructure.

There are relevant subsidies, we need to implement projects promptly. Central government coordinated, local self-government, business, public sector and partner states are the key to successful implementation of all projects, ”the Prime Minister said.

The head of government gave the task of OVA together with the communities to accelerate the filling of the registered property.

Це один із найкращих літаків у світі на сьогодні,переозброїтись яким бажають усі країни, які нині мають на озброєнні F-16. Алеми мусимо тверезо дивитись на теперішній стан речей, і вже давно визначились,який літак ми найреалістичніше можемо отримати, — пояснив він.

Саме літаки типу F-16 є у достатній кількості в багатьох країн-союзниківУкраїни, які вони можуть нам передати та навчити наших пілотів їхзастосовувати. Це є важливою ланкою у створенні української авіаційноїплатформи, літаки поколінь 4+ або 4++ можуть застосовувати різноманітний типозброєнь.

F-16 — це багатоцільовий літак, який може працювати як по повітряних цілях навеликих дистанціях, так і по наземних, зберігаючи при цьому високу мобільністьта оперативність застосування.

Юрій Ігнат також поділився подробицями щодо російських повітряних атак. Зайого словами, ворог почав використовувати керовані авіабомби типу ФАБ-500.

— Власне, окупанти знайшли звичайні фугасні авіаційні бомби ФАБ-500 масою у500 кілограм — це потужна зброя, бомби вільного падіння, які лишають післясебе великі воронки. І причепили до них крила та обладнали GPS-навігацією.Їхні літаки скидають ці бомби поза зоною ураження нашої ППО і уражаютьприфронтові райони, — зазначив речник Повітряних Сил.

Така тактика — це новий виклик для нашої оборони, який ЗСУ мають компенсуватидодатковими комплексами Patriot та SAMP/T. Але найкращий результат можепоказати лише бойовий літак.

— Найефективнішим, зрозуміло, буде F-16, який може застосовувати ракети навідстані до 180 км. Отже, якщо така авіація з’явиться в нас, ми зможемовідганяти російських окупантів далі від наших кордонів, — підсумував ЮрійІгнат.

Glory to Ukraine!

Ukraine received 70 cars for patronage doctors from UNICEF

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-04-06T97:00:00-04:00

Description: Klacksan was detonated by VD Yunisef 70 Automobiliv for Nadannya Drazdoga Dyty by signs ... War with Ukraine 2022, War with Ukraine Latest News today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when, a war with Ukraine In 2022 it will be or not, will there be a war with Ukraine in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukraine’s news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['thumb_202060_820_360_0_0_auto.jpg']

Tags: ['ДЕНИС ШМИГАЛЬ', 'ЮНІСЕФ']

Category: News

Ukraine has received 70 cars from UNICEF to assist children within the birth of at home. The transfer of car to patronage medicines was made with the participation of Prime Minister Denis Shmigal, Minister of Health Victor Lyashko, UNICEF representatives and the Kingdom of the Netherlands.

“Today we strengthen our doctors. Doctors who have special responsibility are the protection of the youngest patients: babies and children up to 3 years. Our children are our future. And today, these words have a special weight of the pupparty. With these words, women gave birth under rocket strokes, and doctors have accepted childbirth. With these words, our military reflect the enemy attacks every day. I express my deep respect and gratitude to our doctors who, despite shelling, rocket and aviation blows, save our people's lives and health. Let these ciavtomobiles serve for the benefit of our country and bring health to children with ribbons, ”the Prime Minister said.

The Head of Government also thanked UNICEF partners, the Kingdom of the Netherlands Tadonoram, whose donations were purchased by cars, reportsGovernment portal.

According to the Prime Minister, thanks to new cars, the government is expanding the project "Caring from Birth at home" to eleven areas. Until now, he worked for three: Zhytomyr, Donetsk, Kirovograd.

During the transfer of cars, the head of the Government also presented thanks to the Cabinet of Ministers of Ukraine to patronage nurses involved in the work of a nuptilo project.

Help: 70 cars purchased at the expense of the UN Children's Fund(UNICEF) (with the support of individual donors of the Kingdom of the Netherlands)Up to 65 primary health care centers in 11 regions of Ukraine(Zhytomyr, Chernihiv, Donetsk, Kharkiv, Kherson, Mykolaiv, Dnipropetrovsk, Kyiv, Zaporizhzhia, as well as Lviv Tarivnensk regions)who were most affected by hostilities and participated in the "Care from Birthday" program .

_ "Caring from home at home" is a joint program of the Ministry of Protection of Nor and UNICEF, which provides for the introduction of a universal-progressive model of home visits to improve the provision of medical and social care to children with 0 to 3 years in primary level.

Ministers discussed the creation of veteran development centers on the basis of educational institutions

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-04-06T98:00:00-04:00

Description: The natives of the regional center of the veteran outlet on the BAZ BAZS BASIV OSVITI, ... War with Ukraine 2022, War with Ukraine Latest News today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when, a war with Ukraine in 2022 Whether there will be a year or not, will there be a war with Ukraine in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukraine’s news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['veteranskyj-biznes.jpg']

Tags: ['ВЕТЕРАНИ ВІЙНИ', 'ВЕТЕРАНСЬКИЙ БІЗНЕС', 'МІНВЕТЕРАНІВ', 'МІНОСВІТИ']

Category: News

The issue of creating regional centers of veterans development on the baseline of education, which will facilitate the reintegration of war veterans, was dedicated to the meeting of the Minister of Education and Science of Ukraine Oksen Lisovy with the Minister of Exercises of Veterans of Ukraine Yulia Laputin.

“For a long time, we will have a call to return to the civilian life of the tauting of our defenders and defenders who are involved today. To overcome this gap, it is now necessary to create veterans reserves. That is, we need to ensure the training of specialists, quality combat participants for their rapid integration. In particular, we have to develop training programs for support and support of veterans, as well as to choose educational establishments, on the basis of which such preparation will be carried out, - said Oleksen Forest.

Yulia Laputina stressed that after Ukraine won in the Russian-Ukrainian war in our country, the second front, economic, with the restoration of the country, would be equally important. That is why the Ministry of Justice is already developing an effective system of transition from a military career to civilian life. One of its main components is the introduction of a system of coordination of vocational adaptation of war veterans, their families and families of fallen defenders, [reports] reportsGovernment portal.

“State veteran policy is not a purely social policy of payments to Higarantia. It is a security policy, economic, cultural and, of course, social. This is an important element of national security. And how high quality reintegration into the society of our defenders and defenders of posting from the war depends on the stability of the Ukrainian state, ”Yulialaputina emphasized.

During the meeting, the parties discussed joint steps to introduce a pilot project of Ministry of Veterans to create veterans development centers. The reconciliation will operate in four regions of Ukraine: Vinnytsia, Dnipropetrovsk, Mykolaiv and Lviv on the basis of defined institutions of higher education. The development of specialists of these HEIs is planned to develop special training programmatic programgia for the support of specialists in the support of war veterans and demobilized persons, as well as for members of their families.The ministers also discussed the creation of conditions for attracting war veterans to act in the field of civic education, national-patriotic tava-patriotic education.

“Our warriors who will return after the victory of Ukraine are a huge potential for the resumption of the country's economy. We support the initiatives of changes and we will do our best to make our interaction fruitful, ”Oksen Lisovyi said.

Negotiation decisions should be made with the participation of Ukraine - White House

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-04-07T-31:13:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-04-07T00:13:00+03:00

Description: The US Administration confirmed the principle that there can be no negotiations in Ukraine without Ukraine, as well as that the Ukrainian leadership should determine the readiness for such negotiations. - Ukrinform.

Images: ["630_360_14546..."]

Tags: ['Переговори', 'США', 'Україна', 'Війна з росією']

Type: Article

The US Administration confirmed the principle that there can be no negotiations on Ukraine of Ukraine, as well as that the Ukrainian leadership should determine the readiness of the negotiations.

This was stated on Thursday during a briefing in Washington Coordinator of the White House Radin Security John Kirby, Ukrinform reports.

“Only President Zelensky can determine whether he is ready, and when he is ready to negotiate, in what context and what. We believe that we cannot be overwhelmed about Ukraine without Ukraine, ”the White House representative said.

Read also:

In this way, he answered the request to comment on the publications with Zakiev's signals that the Ukrainian side was ready to negotiate with the Crimea under certain conditions.

As it was reported, on the eve of influential edition The deputy head of the deputy head of PPO Andriy Sibiga. The Ukrainian official, in particular, stated that Kyiv is ready to discuss with Moscow the future of Crimea, if the assignment reaches the limits of temporarily occupied by the Russians .

"If we manage to achieve our strategic goals on the battlefield, and when we are mugging on the administrative border with the Crimea, we are ready to open a diplomatic page of discussion of this issue," - says the word of a high -ranking representative of PP.

Read also:

At the same time, Sibiga added that in Ukraine they do not exclude the release of Crimea with a military man, says FT.
